<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">British Airways destinations</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>

<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:British_Airways_A380-800_G-XLEC_LHR_2014-03-29.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A British Airways <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Airbus_A380-800" title="Airbus A380-800">Airbus A380-800</a> on short final to <a href="/wiki/Heathrow_Airport" title="Heathrow Airport">Heathrow Airport</a> in 2014.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><a href="/wiki/British_Airways" title="British Airways">British Airways</a> is one of few <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Air_carrier" title="Air carrier">carriers</a> serving destinations across all six inhabited continents. Following is a list of destinations the airline flies to, as of July 2015<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=British_Airways_destinations&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>; terminated destinations are also listed. The list does not include cities served solely by affiliated regional carriers, and some terminated destinations may now be served either via franchise or through <a href="/wiki/Codeshare_agreement" title="Codeshare agreement">codeshare agreements</a> with other carriers. Each destination is provided with the name of the country served, the name of the airport served, and both the <a href="/wiki/International_Air_Transport_Association" title="International Air Transport Association">International Air Transport Association</a> (IATA) three-letter designator (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/IATA_airport_code" title="IATA airport code">IATA airport code</a>) and the <a href="/wiki/International_Civil_Aviation_Organization" title="International Civil Aviation Organization">International Civil Aviation Organization</a> (ICAO) four-letter designator (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ICAO_airport_code" title="ICAO airport code">ICAO airport code</a>).</p>
<p></p>

</ol>
